41003030	Jisas hiykwe senkin sehe me, payhokuaw, homkwe senkin me, hiykwe niohney piap-araw non.
41003031	Jisas so pouh o, nay-ih-nayh o, homkwe sa enekwei sohiy non am-or-ousne. Homkwe ki-apau mon nakrok, sa unsaney prueyn se me-ha, Jisas se lyawriy mekow e. [Mak 6:3; Jon 2:12; Ap 1:14]
41003032	Uwrsa poya-poya homkwe hye liwak sir awndiy kawk, sa homkwe hye senkin mekow, “Hno ipey o, nay-om ine-om o, ki-apau mon lwak, hne pawk.”
41003033	Hiykwe sa senkin lonuayk me, “Hano ipey o, hano nay-om o, posokwaw mo?”
41003034	Hiykwe sa uwrsa hye ma liwak sir awndiy kawk seme lira nok, kiy-me, “Lira e, hano ipey-om, nay-om mokwe, eme.”
41003035	Hano nay-om, ine-om, ipey-om mokwe uwrsa, God so uron ko me ma pyay sohomkwaw.
41004001	Jisas hiykwe uwrsa me mahiy-mon sorasor, howk-ki-someik mon. Uwrsa, hye ma hokruw awndiy kawk mokwe kraiar-ar. Sa hiykwe yeyk kamon mon sehe lwawk wakiawkeyn. Yeyk hokwe howk-iway mon lwak. Uwrsa homkwe sa howk-ki-someik mon swa-hokruw, hu-sane mon. [Mak 3:7-9; Luk 5:1-3]
41004002	Hiykwe omeme kraiar mokwe owhnan-ok non hiymon sorasor. Hiykwe senkin mesor, [Mat 13:34; Mak 4:33-34]
41004003	“Homkwe kwa lonuayk. Enekwei kamon hokwe, uwr prueyn hiykwe wit-i me louh-say e ley.
41004004	Hiy wit-i seme ma louh-say hokwe, har mokwe yerki mon makuayk sakuayk. Sa ahney hom sian-yay sowkriy-a.
41004005	Har mokwe ki, mein non mon makuayk sakuayk, ki sorpay-aw ma kor-wak mon. Peypey pa, wit-i somokwe, yok suw-soma-seyr, payhokuaw ki hokwe sorpay-aw.
41004006	Sawk ey hiy lo menkin, hme lo ian-pa-ian som-kreik. Payhokuaw, homkwe meyk loksow popriy pa.
41004007	Har mokwe ur inan non mo ompok mon makuayk sakuayk. Ur inan non hom swar menkin, sa hme way hoaho, homkwe sa ay leip pa seme lwak.
41004008	Sawk wit-i har mokwe ki yaprue-ar mon makuayk sakuayk. Homkwe yok kei nok, lie nok, ay leip. Ayay mokwe sankaw leip, har mokwe 30, har mokwe 60, har mokwe 100.”
41004009	Sawk hiykwe hme senkin me-kow, “Uwr nweyk non lwak ankin, hiykwe ok seme kwa lonuayk.”
41004010	Sa omok Jisas hiykiaw-aw lwak menkin, hyo ki-wayh o, uwr har hye ma awndiy kawk sohom o, homkwe Jisas se owhnan-ok sohom mo meykyar me mesopok.
41004011	Hiykwe sa hme senkin mekow, “God so yier so ouon-aw-ok kokwe, hme po kow, sawk uwrsa meykyay mon ma lwak somokwe, omeme lowpwarowp mokwe owhnan-ok nonaw lonuayk.
41004012	Suw senkin, ‘Mo hom lira-lira liok e, sawk liy lirway ley. Mo hom lonuayk lonuayk liok e, sawk meykyar mokwe liy nonkway ley. Seyr senkin, homkwe sa hmo uron me kankoum ame, seyr God hiy hmo yor piap-araw me lorionay ha ame.’”
41004013	Jisas hiykwe hmekwe sa senkin mesopok, “Homkwe owhnan-ok okukwe nonkway lwak pey? Senkin lwak ankin, hai, homkwe owhnan-ok har mokwe penkin nonkway ey mo?
41004014	Uwr wit-i me ma lanio ouh-say sohokwe, God so ok me lanio ouh-say.
41004015	Uwrsa har homkwe wit-i yerki mon ma makuayk sakuayk me hieyn. Hom kiy-nuw-onuayk nonaw, Satan hiykwe le nok, ok hmo uron mon ma louh-say seme lonokyaw ok.
41004016	Uwrsa har homkwe wit-i, ki mein non mon ma makuayk sakuayk me hieyn. Hom ok ke kiy-nuw-onuayk nonaw, homkwe kar nonaw nak-onok.
41004017	Sawk hom meyk loksow pa ma lwak me hokuaw kokwe, homkwe enekwei meipey seyn lwak pey. Hme mon yorpayor ankin, seyr hom low non lwak ankin, homkwe makuayk sakuayk lira por ha.
41004018	Uwrsa har homkwe, wit-i ur inan non mo ompok mon makuayk sakuayk me hieyn. Somokwe God so ok ke ma lonuayk hom non.
41004019	Sawk homkwe yor kraiar ki ko me nan kworpakwor, seyr omeme kraiar nak-wayr e ma lira way o, seyr omeme har me ma nan koukou-ay o, sohom lyawriy-sawriy mon kane kawk, sa homkwe ay leip pa seme lwak. [Mat 19:23-24]
41004020	Sawk uwrsa har homkwe wit-i ki yaprue mon ma makuayk sakuayk me hieyn. Homkwe ok ke lonuayk nok, lonok nok, ay leip ok. Har homkwe 30, har homkwe 60, har homkwe 100.”
41004021	Seyr Jisas hiy hme makiy-me, “Hai, uwr prueyn hiykwe lam se yowr ouon o, sey liawon ey ko ouon o, serey pankaw loum pukyay nak-kwawk o? Korey, sawk hiykwe lam sohokwe sey ayaw mon nak-yay yar. [Mat 5:15; Luk 11:33]
41004022	Ompay ompay ma lwak sue mokwe, kumay mon ya nak-ousne sa-ousne a. Seyr ompay ompay ma nak-sapos sapos sue mokwe, ya leyp-say hrahra ha a. [Mat 10:26; Luk 12:2]
41004023	Uwr nweyk non lwak ankin, hiykwe ok seme kwa lonuayk.”
41004024	Seyr hiy me, “Ok hom ma lonuayk mokwe, kwa nanpanan popriy. Meir, hom uwrsa har me ma lira sor anon non kokwe, God hiykwe seyr hme kokwe meir sohom nonaw lira sor anon ey, seyr ipey-ar manak-kow ey. [Mat 7:2]
41004025	Uwr prueyn hiykwe payay me nak-wayr e, hye kokwe kraiar manak-kow peykyay. Sawk uwr prueyn hiykwe puraw-ar nuw-wak ankin, sawk hiy payay se kornak-wayr e, sohokwe seyr ma-kahya.” [Mat 13:12; 25:29; Luk 19:26]
41004026	Jisas hiy makiy-me, “God so Wayr-hre-yier hokwe, uwr prueyn, ayay-i ki mon ma louh-say sian me hieyn.
41004027	Arawh enekwei hokwe, hiykwe anwaw liawon nayr. Eypok hokwe hiykwe loksian anio kok. Enekwei sohokwe, ayay-i somokwe, yok kei lousne sa-ousne ie, sawk hiykwe ayay-i sohom penkin kei lousne sa-ousne e, hiykwe nonkway lopa.
41004028	Ayay-yok mokwe mo ki hiykiaw-aw mon eyr ie, ayay leip sawan kreik nok. Peyr, yok iwon hiy lousne pie, sei, ku hiy lie nok, simonpiy hiy lore ok.
41004029	Simonpiy hom aiopey-hay lwak ankin, uwr sohokwe seik ke lonok nok, simonpiy seme ompan kawk ok. Payhokuaw, ayay la enekwei hokwe papo lousne.” [Jol 3:13; MHO 14:15]
41004030	Jisas hiy ma-me, “God so Wayr-hre-yier hokwe, penkin so, hromkwe penkin kiy-me ey so? Hromkwe owhnan-ok penkin ke kiy-me memeir o?
41004031	God so Wayr-hre-yier hokwe, mastet-i * se hieyn. Mastet-i hokwe, ayay-i lowpwarowp ki mon ma saro mo paswaw-ar.
41004032	Sawk hye ki mon saro ankin, hiykwe kei ie nok, ayay lowpwarowp wueir ko mo aiopey-hay-ar nuw-wak, seyr kueim aiopey-hay non nuw-wak. Sa ahney ayaw ko homkwe, hne, hyo kueim-eykos mon sian-yay sowkriy meio iawon sowkway ok.”
41004033	Jisas hiykwe uwrsa me kokwe owhnan-ok kraiar liyliy-aw senkin non mesor kow. Seyr hiykwe hom nonkway ey mo limon nonaw mesor kow.
41004034	Hiykwe uwrsa me kokwe ok kamon owhnan-ok lopa mesor kow pa. Sawk enekwei hiy hyo ki-wayh arian me nion-aw non-wak menkin, hiykwe ok lowpwarowp mo meykyar mokwe sohiy non mesor kow.
41004035	Eypok sohiy so eyrowpwar hokwe, Jisas hiy hyo ki-wayh me kiy-me, “Ama, hromkwe karayh menki mon lokuan e.”
41004036	Homkwe uwrsa popua hay me lokriy hain nok, yeyk hiy ma wakiawkeyn serey lwawk. Yeyk har seyn, hme nion siraw non-hiok kuan.
41004037	Sa howniy aiopey hay hok pa kiynuw-way huwhuw oksian, seyr hu-par hom kiy-nuw-oksian swa-popapop swanon-kwawk, yeyk mon. Sa yeyk-hu hokwe pau woki nuw-wak ohriar.
41004038	Jisas hiykiaw kokwe yeke mon lwon kwawk, mawk-sow eir mon. Homkwe sa hye kanwei sian nok, hye senkin kiy-me, “Hakamay ara, hreme pa lopruw ley, hunkwe hreme uron pankaw lowk o?”
41004039	Jisas hiykwe loksian nok, howniy ke me-hripahri, seyr hu-par me senkin kiynak-me, “Sopiaw, kwa kueyn-yay.” Seseyn, howniy hok lon-kane nok, hu-par hok nonyo keyn.
41004040	Jisas hiykwe sa hyo ki-wayh me senkin kiy-mekow, “Homkwe panoke hok o? Homkwe nan kiykiy-ay lopa lwak nonaw nuw-wak o?”
41004041	Homkwe sa hok, sa homkiaw-ayay senkin seme lohruw, “Uwr ohokwe penkin uwr so? Mo howniy hi, hu-par hi, hyo ok me lonuayk me.”
41005001	Sa homkwe howk-menki mon lokin peykyay, Gerasa mo kipay mon.
41005002	Jisas hiy yeyk se lokriy hain menkin, uwr prueyn niohney piap-araw non hiykwe hye lonyay huon e le. Hiykwe uwrsa-sopok me lopru linon kreik yier ko se le.
41005003	Hiykwe uwrsa-sopok me lopru inon kreik yier mon-aw lwayr, seyr uwr prueyn hye liy ma-way-pruwmapruw orok ley. Mo ihey mo mays sen non hi, liy-ar so.
41005004	Hyo sune-iha mokwe, enekwei kraiar sen non po sakreik lokruok, sawk hiykwe enekwei enekwei, sen me leyma-say nok, ain hyo sune ko me okima-kei say ok. Uwr prueyn, krai non hye way-pruwmapruw yay ey hokwe korey lwak pa.
41005005	Eypok-arawh eypok arawh, hiykwe uwrsa-sopok me lopru inon kreik yier mon o, mnuw mon o, serey-aw lanio weyr-weyr wonkawk wonkawk wayr, seyr hyo owh arian se nak-ei prumapru, mein non.
41005006	Hiy Jisas se ma lira huon hokwe, hiykwe meiaw-ar kor-wak, hiykwe sa sau ne nok, Jisas so inour mon pamuow kampueys.
41005007	Seyr wouk-ok aiopey non senkin nuwnak-weyr-weyr me, “Jisas, God Seirpey Ayaw-ar ko so Ney, hunkwe hane penkin lon ley? Hakwe hne God se hokuaw senkin mesopok, hunkwe hane aw ipey-ar peie mon ok o!” [Mak 1:24]
41005008	Hiykwe senkin sehe me, payhokuaw Jisas hiykwe senkin me, “Niohney piap-araw, uwr ohiy so owh ko se ar-ousne ha e!”
41005009	Jisas hiy hye mesopok, “Hno uru hokwe poho?” Hiy mekow, “Hano uru hokwe, Ami, payhokuaw, hromkwe ompuay!”
41005010	Seyr hiykwe Jisas se hme kipay kamon mon mesu-ha lopa lwak e hrousohrou nuw-onseyn kraiay.
41005011	Huok orhey non hokwe mnuw-pawk ohriar serey lanio sayok-a.
41005012	Sa niohney piap-araw somokwe Jisas se senkin lonseyn, “Hunkwe hreme huok mo owh mon me-ha nok, hreme nak-isay yawriy, huok mo swaw mon.”
41005013	Sa Jisas hiykwe hme ipan seme lon ha. Homkwe sa uwr sehe lokriy hain nok, huok mo owh mon lyawriy-sawriy. Huok somokwe sa mnuw-pawk ma ar-okin sapruw kawk nok mon seme nak-onsau onsau kumey ondeys ondeys pruw lowpway. Huok sohom mo meir hokwe sankaw, 2000.
41005014	Huok-kow-a-uwr homkwe sa hakan sakan nok nok, ok sokwe yier aiopey hay mon o, om paswaw yier aiopey sohiy so meykyay mon ma lwak sohom o, hme nuw-mesor nakian nakian kow ha. Uwrsa homkwe sa seme ley neyney ira, weynpaweyn serey ma lousne ke.
41005015	Hom Jisas so owh mon lousne menkin, homkwe sa uwr, paraw niohney piap-araw kraiar non liok hiy wakiawkeyn se lira. Hiykwe omeme owh ko po lie, seyr hyo mawkhow hokwe, yaprue po ma-lwak. Homkwe sa seme nuw-hok.
41005016	Uwrsa me kokwe, yor, uwr niohney piap-araw non se ma lousne o, huok o, uwr ma lira ha hom mesor kow.
41005017	Homkwe sa Jisas se sehe lonseyn, hmo kipay se lokriy hain e.
41005018	Jisas hiy yeyk mon lwawk menkin, uwr paraw niohney piap-araw non ma lwak liok, hiykwe sa Jisas se lonseyn, hiy siraw non-ey e.
41005019	Sawk Jisas hiykwe hye ipan lon pa, sa hiykwe hye senkin mekow, “Hunkwe a mon ley nok, hne Hakamay hiy pankaw hiy-mon e, seyr uron penkin lowk e, seme hno nioh siraw-aw me kwa mesor kow.”
41005020	Uwr sohokwe sa sehe ley nok, yor, Jisas hiy hye ma hiymon ke Dekapolis mo kipay lowpwarowp mon lanio mesor kow. Uwrsa ma lonuayk homkwe sa uron preiryay.
41005021	Jisas hiy howk-menki mon ma-lokuan menkin, uwrsa popua-hay homkwe, hyo owh mon nuw-hokruw, howk ki-someik mon.
41005022	Juda mo hokruw-a so hakamay prueyn, Jairus, hiykwe serey le. Hiy Jisas se lira menkin, hiykwe Jisas so sune mon makuayk nok,
41005023	Jisas se senkin lonseyn kraiay, “Hano ney swanyo nopre hokwe pau lokrue ohriar lwak. Hunkwe hno iha me hoko owh mon kekie e, sa hokwe yaprue ka lwak, seyr su ka lwayr.”
41005024	Jisas hiykwe sa hye nion sehe non-ey. Uwrsa popua-hay hom seyn, siraw nwakwon nwakwon ey, seyr Jisas se nuw-awndiy kawk.
41005025	Sa prueyn hokwe serey non-wak. Hokwe nioh yia sankaw po ley wayr-wayr, iha seys mu nareysyar.
41005026	Hokwe dokta kraiar mo owh mon po nakey, seyr hoko mein-owon lowpwarowp po sasow lowpway. Sawk hok yaprue lwak e ma mon kokwe, hokwe enekwei enekwei piaparaw-ar nuw-wak.
41005027	Hokwe Jisas se ma mesor me lonuayk menkin, hokwe hyo meyki mon uwrsa mo ompok-aw ley nok, hyo saket ke sapou.
41005028	Payhokuaw, hokwe nanpanan, “Hakwe hyo owh ko omeme me-aw sapou ankin, hakwe yaprue po lwak a.”
41005029	Hoko nioh hokwe sa enekwei sohiy nonaw kiynuw-onkane, seyr hokwe senkin lokinhre ir, hoko low kokwe po mon popriy kow.
41005030	Enekwei sohiy nonaw kokwe, Jisas hiykwe senkin nonkway, hyo krai har homkwe hye po lokriy hain. Hiykwe sa uwrsa mo ompok ko se swahre nok, senkin mesopok, “Hano owh ko omeme mokwe, posokwaw sapou so?” [Luk 6:19]
41005031	Hyo ki-wayh hom lonuayk me, “Hunkwe uwrsa hne ma awndiy kawk seme lira e, hai, hunkwe senkin panoke mesopok o, hne posokwaw sapou so?”
41005032	Sawk Jisas hiykwe unsaney, hye ma sapou se lira e swahre-ahre ira nonaw lwak.
41005033	Sa sokukwe weynpaweyn hoko owh mon ma lousne ke lira nonkway menkin, hokwe hok non nak-kowkow ne nok, hye pamuow kampueys nok, ok-ar ke nuw-me-hrorsay kow lowpway.
41005034	Jisas hiy hoke me, “Ney akwa, hno uron hane ma nanpanan kiykiy-ay hiykiaw-aw, hne po mon popriy kow. Hunkwe liwak marowhway yor non-aw kwa nakey e, seyr hno low hokwe hne ka lokriy hain.” [Mak 10:52; Luk 7:50; 17:19]
41005035	Jisas hiy lohruw-a non-aw, uwr har Jairus so a ko homkwe le nok, Jairus se mekow, “Hno ney hokwe papo lokrue. Hiy-mon-sorasor-uwr se panoke ma-mon sese-yay o?”
41005036	Jisas hiykwe hmo ok somokwe, lonuayk lopa, sawk Juda mo hokruw-a so hakamay se kiy-me, “Hunkwe peie hok o, kwahnaw nanpanan kiykiy-ay e.”
41005037	Hiykwe uwrsa har me hye nion non-ey e ipan lon lopa, sawk Pita o, Jems o, Jems so nay-ih Jon o, hme-aw me-huonokyaw nok.
41005038	Hom Jairus so a mon lousne menkin, Jisas hiykwe uwrsa hom moryak moryak me amor-ira. Homkwe eheyr aiopey hay nuw-yuk, seyr eheyr-yowp aiopey hay lyuk me.
41005039	Hiy lyawriy nok, hme me, “Homkwe panoke nuw-moryak moryak o? Homkwe eheyr panoke lyuk o? Ney okukwe lokrue pa, hokwe anwaw liawon.”
41005040	Homkwe sawk hye kweyr kow. Hiykwe sa uwrsa me ki-apau mon seme me-su ha. Hiykwe sa-ney ko orih pouh uwrsa o, hyo ki-wayh pruompri-ar o, senkinaw huonok nok, ampok, ney hok ma liawon mon hiy-yawriy.
41005041	Jisas hiykwe sa-ney sohok ko iha ke nekie nok, hoke kiy-me, “Talita kum.” Ok sohok ko meyk-ar kokwe senkin, “Sa-ney paswaw akwa, hakwe hne me, loksian e.” [Luk 7:14]
41005042	Enekwei sohiy nonaw kokwe sa-ney sokukwe loksian nok, a mon lanio kwawk. Hoko yia mokwe sankaw, iha seys, mu nareysyar.
41005043	Sawk Jisas hiykwe hom unsaney me mesor kow ame kiynak-me-sous kupaku nok, hme me, sa-ney sokwe ayay har kow-a e.
41006001	Jisas hiykwe yier sehe lokriy hain nok, hyo om arian mon ma-ley, hyo ki-wayh me nion.
41006002	Sabat-enekwei lwak menkin, hiykwe Juda mo hokruw-a mon uwrsa me God so ok me mesor kow. Uwrsa kraiar homkwe hye lonuayk menkin, homkwe senkin kowkow-yay mesopok, “Ok yaprue somokwe, hiykwe perey suko me lonok mo? Mawkhow ihey-ar hye ma kow mokwe, penkin mo? Hiykwe meir krai non mokwe, penkin meio o? [Jon 7:15]
41006003	Uwr sohokwe a meio uwr hiykwaw, hiykwe Maria ko ney. Hyo uwrku mokwe hreme nion lwak. Hyo nay-ih-nayh Jems, Josep, Judas, Saimon om homkwe. Hyo ine-ih nayh seyn.” Homkwe senkin me menkin, sawk hye sehe me-puar.
41006004	Jisas hiy hme kiy-me, “Profet sekwe uru ayaw mon ma lwak hokwe, yier lowpwarowp har hom kow, sawk hyo yier arian o, hyo uwrku arian o, hyo nioh siraw-aw o, hom korey.” [Jon 4:44]
41006005	Hiykwe meir krai non mokwe, yier serey mon kokwe, liy meio ley. Sawk peik-uwr har-har-aw me-aw hyo iha non nekie sasowriy sow kow.
41006006	Hiykwe kowkow-yay, payhokuaw uwrsa homkwe nan kiykiy-ay pa. Jisas hiykwe sa yier har ohriar ma lwak me ley sor kow.
41006007	Hiykwe hyo ki-wayh iha seys mu nareysyar non me me-huonok nok, prueys seyn, prueys seyn, senkin me-ha, seyr krai niohney piap-araw me me-su ha ey se nak-kow ha.
41006008	Hiykwe sawk hme senkin me-kupaku popriy ha, “Hmo lanio mokwe, irowm me-aw nakey, omeme senkin senkin lopa, ihey mo naw lopa, owk lopa, owk-neyp meinowon non lopa.
41006009	Sune-owhi me-aw lie nakey, sawk owh ko omeme ohna non peie nakey o.”
41006010	Hiy hme nak-me kow, “Hme a perey me-huonok yawriy e, serey-aw lwayr, hom yier sehe lokriy hain.
41006011	Yier, hme me-huonok yawriy pa lwak ankin, seyr hme lonuayk pa lwak ankin, homkwe yier sehe lokriy hain nok, kosi-pow hmo sune ko me kiy-our powpow say hain. Sohokwe meir, yier sehe ma lono hiy non.” [Luk 10:4-11; Ap 13:51]
41006012	Ki-wayh homkwe sa seme ley neyney mesor kow, uwrsa hom uron kankoum e.
41006013	Homkwe niohney piap-araw kraiar me me-su ha, seyr uwrsa kraiar peik non me wel non low mon popriy kow. [Je 5:14]
41006014	King Herot hiykwe sa mey lowpwarowp seme lonuayk, payhokuaw Jisas sekwe om serey serey po mesor nakian nakian. Uwrsa har homkwe senkin me, “Jon, hu mon prouk uwr hiykwe ki-eyh ko se po ma-loksian. Hiykwe krai, meir krai non me meio ey non sehe lwak.” [Mat 16:14; Mak 8:28; Luk 3:19-20]
41006015	Har hom sawk senkin me, “Hiykwe Elaija.” Wo, har homkwe sa senkin me, “Hiykwe profet, profet paraw-uh mo prueyn se hieyn.”
41006016	Herot hiy lonuayk menkin, hiy me, “Ohokwe Jon, hu mon prouk uwr, uwr hyo hei se ha ma lokiane sow hiy non, sawk hiykwe po ma-loksian.”
41006017	Jon sekwe mo Herot hiykiaw me-sasay nekie nok, sen non sakawk nok, kalabus-a mon nak-okin sakawk. Hiykwe senkin kokwe Herodias, hyo nay-ih so sah, hiy ma huon ke hokuaw mon.
41006018	Payhokuaw, Jon, hu mon prouk uwr hiykwe Herot se senkin mekow wayr, “Weynpaweyn sokukwe piap-araw, hwon hno nay Filip so sah ke ma huon sohokwe.” [Wkp 18:16]
41006019	Sa Herodias hokwe, Jon se kokwe kasaw sokwe hohuaw, seyr hye lokin kwor okrue e sokwe mon, sawk hokwe liy so.
41006020	Payhokuaw, Herot hiykwe Jon se hok. Hiykwe senkin nonkway, Jon hiykwe uwr yaprue, seyr pekneyweys, sa hiykwe Jon se sehe hiy-mon sosor. Hiykwe Jon so ok mokwe, aiopey hay nanpanan kworpakwor kawk, sawk hiykwe lonuayk e mon.
41006021	Sa omok-ar, enekwei kamon Herodias hok yaprue ma lira hiy lousne. Enekwei sohokwe, Herot se ma liwak hiy non. Enekwei sohokwe, Herot hiykwe hyo uwr hakamay o, hyo aw-uwr mo hakamay o, peyrmawk liarok-uwr Galili ko o, hme ayay kraiar lunay kekie kow.
41006022	Herodias ko ney swanyo hokwe lyawriy nok, owk lowk. Herot o, uwr, ayay hye nion ma non-iwak sir a, homkwe kar ley. King hiykwe sa hoke sokwe me, “Hunkwe pay me lonok e nan o? Hakwe hne kow ey.”
41006023	Hiykwe hoke kokwe, kraiar senkin loiow me-sakon kawk, “Hakwe senkin loiow, hwon pay-ay se mesopok e, hakwe hne kow ey, mo kipay, ha ma hiy-wayr so kopi aiopey hay hi.”
41006024	Sa-ney sokukwe hoko pouh ko owh mon ma-ley nok mesopok, “Hakwe pay me kiy-mesopok o?” Pouh hok lonuayk me, “Jon, hu mon prouk uwr so makwey se mesopok e.”
41006025	Sa-ney sokukwe king so owh mon masaw-ey nok, omnuw-me, “Hane kokwe Jon so makwey se pokon-awaw plet mon lokiane kwawk nakway kow e.”
41006026	King hiykwe sa uron aiopey hay nuw-owk kworpakwor kawk. Sawk hiy ma loiow o, uwrsa hye nion ma non-iwak sir a o, seme hokuaw kokwe, hiykwe hoke liy me-puar ley.
41006027	Sei, hiykwe sa aw-uwr prueyn se sehe kiysaw-me-sasay ha, Jon so makwey se nake kow e. Aw-uwr sohokwe kalabus-a mon ley nok, Jon so makwey se lokiane sow.
41006028	Hiykwe makwey sohokwe plet non kwawk nake nok, sa-ney sokwe nakway kow. Hokwe sa pouh ke ma-sahre nakway kow.
41006029	Jon so ki-wayh hom lonuayk menkin, homkwe le nok, hyo owhi-sopok ke lway opru kwawk.
41006030	Aposel hom Jisas so mon ma-le-nene nok, mey lowpwarowp hom ma meio o, ma hiymon sorasor o, seme hye mesor kow. [Luk 10:17]
41006031	Sa uwrsa kraiar hom eriey ley, erey le, senkin ma lon me hokuaw kokwe, Jisas o, hyo ki-wayh o, homkwe ayay enekwei korey korey kiy-a ley. Sa Jisas hiykwe hyo ki-wayh me seme me, “Hromkwe hromkiaw-aw yier kamon mon ley neyney e, sa homkwe serey liwak nieys ey.”
41006032	Homkwe sa yeyk non homkiaw-aw seme ley neyney, yier kamon unsaney lopa mon.
41006033	Sawk uwrsa kraiar homkwe hom ma ley neyney mokwe, po lira ha, seyr po lira nonkway. Sa uwrsa yier lowpwarowp ko homkwe kiaw kiaw-aw seme lonsau onsau nok, sa yier, Jisas hiy ma hiy-ey mon peyrmawk lousne sa-ousne pie.
41006034	Jisas hiy yeyk ko se wakeyn menkin, hiykwe sa uwrsa popua hay me lira. Hiykwe sa hme uron lowk, payhokuaw, homkwe sipsip naykih lopa me hieyn. Hiykwe sa pau, hme ok kraiar kiy-hiynuw-mon-sorasor. [Nam 27:17; Mat 9:36]
41006035	Arawh po serey kiy-wak a, hyo ki-wayh homkwe hyo owh mon le nok, me, “Enekwei hokwe pau arawh ohriar kiy-wak, seyr yier ohokwe unsaney lopa. [Mak 8:1-9]
41006036	Uwrsa me me-ha e, homkwe wueir-om o, yier o, ohriar erey ma lwak mon ayay ka ley neyney nakway a.
41006037	Sawk Jisas hiykwe senkin lonuayk me, “Homkiaw kiy-kow-a e.” Hom mesopok, “Hunkwe hrom ihey mo naw 200 Silva non nakway nok, uwrsa eme kow-a, senkin lon e me o?”
41006038	Hiy hme mesopok, “Homkwe ihey mo naw mokwe, pankaw mo? Kwa ley ira.” Hom ley sor ir nok, hye mekow, “Ihey mo naw iha sirom, ay ireys.”
41006039	Sei, Jisas hiy hyo ki-wayh me me, uwrsa me hou non hou non pan eir mon me-say kikrweik e.
41006040	Uwrsa homkwe sa senkin seme kikrweik, hou har 100, hou har 50.
41006041	Jisas hiy ihey mo naw iha sirom o, ay ireys-ar o, seme lonokyaw nok, nonkumey mon ar-nak-ira nok, God se nak-me-ihey. Hiykwe ihey mo naw seme kamane nok, hyo ki-wayh me kow, uwrsa me lowndiy kow e. Hiykwe seyr ay ireys-ar sokwe hme lowpwarowp me nak-kamaun kow.
41006042	Uwrsa lowpwarowp hom la menkin, homkwe swaw liy nuwnak-wak.
41006043	Ki-wayh homkwe ihey mo naw o, ay ireys-ar o, seme ma la prue mokwe, yowr iha seys, mu nareysyar, sankaw kawk kreik prusow.
41006044	Uwr ayay seme ma la mo meir hokwe, 5000.
41006045	Jisas hiykwe hyo ki-wayh me yeyk mon kiy-saw-mon wawk nok, Betsaida, howk-menki mon ma lwak mon kuan naruok e me-ha. Hiykwe peyr uwrsa me me-ha.
41006046	Hiy uwrsa me me-ihey ha nok, mnuw mon ley, God se mesopok e. [Luk 5:16]
41006047	Eyrowpwar lwak menkin, yeyk hokwe, howk-iway ompok sok lwak, Jisas hiykwe hiykiaw-aw ki mon lwak.
41006048	Hiykwe sa senkin lira, hyo ki-wayh homkwe, youk nuw-hiok lokruok, payhokuaw, howniy hokwe hom ma ley senkin hremon ka-kaye. Sa enekwei 3 klok o, 6 klok o, enekwei sohiy so ompok sok lwak nerie menkin, hiykwe hmo owh mon lousne, hu eir mon lanio ne. Hiykwe hme ka-swaneyk ney e nan.
41006049	Sawk homkwe hiy hu eir mon lanio se lira, “Ohokwe poup,” hom nanpanan, sa homkwe seme nuw-weyr-weyr. [Luk 24:37]
41006050	Hom lowpwarowp hye lira huon menkin, homkwe nuw-hok krwepakrwe kawk. Sa hmekwe Jisas hiykiaw kiy-saw-me, “Krai lwak e, ohokwe hakiaw. Peie hok o.”
41006051	Sei, hiy hme nion yeyk mon non-wawk, seyr howniy hok lonkane. Ki-wayh homkwe aiopey hay nuw-nanpanan kworpakwor kawk. [Mak 4:39]
41006052	Payhokuaw, homkwe 5000 uwr me ma kow-a so meyk-ar hokwe, korey nonkway pa. Hmo uron mokwe po mon kraipakrai yay.
41006053	Hom howk ke lokuan nok, sa Genesaret mon lokin peykyay. Yeyk hokwe homkwe serey piynay.
41006054	Hom yeyk ko me wakeyn sakeyn nonaw, uwrsa homkwe Jisas se po saw-ira nonkway.
41006055	Sa homkwe kipay lowpwarowp serey ma lwak mon lonsau onsau nok, sa hom hiy perey lwak se lonuayk e, homkwe peik-uwrsa sey non ma linon nok mokwe, serey nakey.
41006056	Jisas hiy perey ley me, hiy yier mon ley, om aiopey hay mon ley, wueir-om mon ley, unsaney homkwe uwrsa peik non mokwe, ayay-nakway-yier mon lway nakey neyney. Homkwe Jisas se lonseyn, hyo saket ko kopi ke-aw uwrsa peik non me ipan lon sapou e. Sa lowpwarowp hye ma sapou homkwe, yaprue ma-lwak.
41007001	Farisi * o, sow ke hiymon-sorasor uwr har o, Jerusalem ko me ma le nene homkwe, Jisas se am-nuw-awndiy kawk.
41007002	Homkwe senkin lira, Jisas so ki-wayh har homkwe, ayay mokwe, iha orki non nak-a. Suw senkin, homkwe iha mokwe sow hok ma me senkin peyryapeyr pa. [Luk 11:38]
41007003	(Payhokuaw, Farisi o, Juda uwrsa lowpwarowp o, homkwe hmo iwey-om hom ma hiymon sorasor me pyay. Homkwe ayay liy saw-a ley, peyr hmo iha me peyryapeyr, hmo sow hok ma me senkin.)
41007004	Homkwe ayay nakway yier ko me ma-le-nene ankin, homkwe ayay liy la ley, hom hu perey hawr. Seyr homkwe sow har kraiar hom ma lonok me nak-pyay. Sow senkin, yiawk o, sospen o, hu-yiawk aiopey hay o, seme peyryapeyr yor. [Mat 23:25]
41007005	Farisi o, sow ke hiymon sorasor uwr o, homkwe sa Jisas se sehe mesopok, “Hai, hno ki-wayh homkwe hromo iwey-om hom ma hiymon sorasor hain me pyay pa, panoke lwak o? Wo, homkwe ayay mokwe sawk iha orki non nak-a.”
41007006	Jisas hiy lonuayk me, “Okrei-uwr om, Aisaia hiykwe mo okar me, hiy hme profet-ok non senkin ma mey hokwe, ‘Uwrsa omokwe, hano uru hokwe woki nonaw lowk nakie, sawk hmo uron mokwe hano meiaw mon lwak.
41007007	Homkwe hane puraw nuw-kampueys me-ihey lokruok. Seyr hmo sow arian hom ma hiymon sorasor somokwe, homkwe senkin nak-me-loior kow, somokwe God so sow arian.’
41007008	Homkwe God so me-kupaku-ok mokwe po lokriy ha, sa homkwe uwr ki ko mo sow me nakruok.”
41007009	Jisas hiy hme ma-me, “Hom hmo sow arian me pyay e, God so me-kupaku-ok me meykyay mon ma kekie mokwe, homkwe yerki yaprue-ar non.
41007010	Payhokuaw, Moses hiykwe senkin me, ‘Hunkwe hno ipey-aio me yaprue kwa nan ihey,’ seyr, ‘Uwr hyo ipey-aio me posokwaw hruo-yay kow e, hyekwe kwa lokin kwor okrue.’
41007011	Sawk homkwe uwrsa me kokwe yor piap kamon ke senkin hiy-mon sorasor, ney homkwe hmo ipey, aio leys se liy nak-me kow, ‘Ipey, aio leys ama, hakwe hehe liy hiymon ley, payhokuaw, omeme hano, hehe ma hiymon ey mokwe, hakwe korban-ok po me.’” (Ok “korban” sohok ko meyk-ar hokwe senkin, maym, God se kow ey hok non).
41007012	“Suw homkwe, uwrsa hom hmo ipey-aio me hiymon ey hokwe, ipan lon pey.
41007013	Hiymon sorasor-ok hom uwrsa har me ma kow somokwe, sa God so ok ke ouon mon kyor-our seipasei ha, hmo apaw-om mo sow arian me-aw lowk nakie e. Seyr homkwe yor kraiar liyliy-aw senkin mokwe, senaw mon.”
41007014	Jisas hiy uwrsa popua hay me ma-me-huonok nok, me, “Hom lowpwarowp kokwe hane kwa lonuayk, seyr kwa nak-nonkway.
41007015	Omeme kamon kumay ko unsaney prueyn so swaw mon ma lyawriy hokwe, unsaney sehe liy mon orpar orpar yay ley. Sawk unsaney se ma mon orpar orpar hokwe, omeme hyo uron ko me ma lousne homkwaw.” * [Ap 10:14-15]
41007017	Hiy uwrsa popua hay seme lokriy hain, sa a mon lyawriy menkin, hyo ki-wayh homkwe sa owhnan-ok sohok ko meykyar ke mesopok.
41007018	Jisas hiy hme me, “Hmo nonkway mokwe, uwrsa har mo nonkway mo eir mon lwak pey. Homkwe nuw-nonkway pey? Mon kamon kumay ko unsaney so mon ma lyawriy hokwe, hye liy mon orki orki ley.
41007019	Payhokuaw, mon sohokwe, uron mon lyawriy pey, sawk swaw mon lyawriy nok, hyo owh ko se ma-lousne ok.” (Jisas hiy senkin ma me hokwe, hiykwe senkin me-kumay, ayay lowpwarowp mokwe, orki lopa.)
41007020	Hiy ma-me, “Uwrsa mo uron ko pay-ay hiykwaw lousne e, sohiykwaw mon orki orki.
41007021	Payhokuaw, uwrsa mo uron ko mokwe, yor enkin hom lousne sa-ousne: nanpanan yor piap-araw o, yor orki non o, yokun yor o, unsaney lokin kwor yor o, yokun nweyh kane yor o,
41007022	ompreir kawk yor o, yor piap senkin senkin o, okrei yor o, powey powey yor o, lira way ompeys-ma-peys yor o, me-kawrpakawr yor o, nak-me-heyr yor o, owk lapala yor o.
41007023	Yor piap lowpwarowp somokwe uron ouon ko me lousne, seyr uwrsa me mon orki-orki-yay.”
41007024	Jisas hiykwe yier sehe lokriy hain nok, Tair mo kipay mon ley. Hiykwe sa a kamon mon lyawriy. Hiykwe hiy serey ma lwak hokwe, uwrsa hom nonkway e mon pa. Sawk hiykwe liy lwak sue ley.
41007025	Sa prueyn, hoko ney swanyo niohney piap-araw non hok Jisas hiy ma lwak se lonuayk menkin, hokwe saw-e nok, hyo sune mon makuayk.
41007026	Sa sokukwe uwrkayn irweyk ko. Hekekwe kipay Fonisia, Siria mon ma lwak mon liwak. Hokwe Jisas se lonseyn, niohney piap-araw hoko ney ko owh mon ma lwak se me-su ha e.
41007027	Sawk Jisas hiykwe senkin lonuayk me, “Peyr hromkwe ney me kow-a e. Ney mo ayay me nwoh me lomuwn say kow yor sokukwe yaprue korey.” *
41007028	Sa sohok lonuayk me, “Hakamay ara, mo nwoh tebol ouon ko hi, homkwe ney mo ayay somei me la.”
41007029	Jisas hiykwe sa hoke senkin mekow, “Hwon senkin ma ma-sahre me ko hokuaw kokwe, hunkwe kwa ley e, niohney piap-araw hokwe, hno ney ke po lokriy hain.”
41007030	Hok a mon ley nok, sa ney hok yop liawon ey mon liawon ke lira. Niohney piap-araw hokwe, hoke po lokriy hain.
41007031	Sohiy so meyki hokwe, Jisas hiykwe Tair mo kipay se lokriy hain nok, sa Saidon mo kipay mon ley hain, sei, sa howk Galili mon seyn kyor-okumey, Dekapolis mo kipay mon.
41007032	Unsaney har homkwe uwr prueyn ma lonuayk lopa, seyr ok ma me lopa se hyo owh mon hiy-e. Sa homkwe hye lonseyn, hyo iha ke uwr sohiy so owh mon kekie e.
41007033	Jisas hiy uwr sehe kiy-huonok nok, uwrsa popua hay mo meiaw mon hiy-ey. Hiykwe hyo yodne se uwr sohiy so nweyk mon ka-lok-ha nok, somor somor-say nok, uwr sohiy so sane se sapou.
41007034	Sei, Jisas hiykwe nonkumey mon ar-ira nok, lenieys kawk nok, uwr sehe senkin kiy-me, “Efata.” Ok sohok ko meyk-ar hokwe senkin, “Lon-kampi e.”
41007035	Enekwei sohiy nonaw kokwe, uwr sohiy so nweyk hom kiynuw-on-kamapi, seyr hyo sane hiy kiy-nuw-on-kansopra ha. Sa hiykwe ok yaprue me sasowriy sow ha.
41007036	Sei, Jisas hiy hom uwrsa har me ma-mesor kow ame nak-me kupaku me-sous, sawk hiy hme kraiar ma me-kupaku hokwe, homkwe kraiar-ar nuw-mesor. [Mak 1:43-45]
41007037	Uwrsa ma lonuayk homkwe nuw-preiryay. Hom me, “Hiykwe mey lowpwarowp mokwe yaprue po nuw-meio. Hiykwe uwr ma lonuayk lopa me mon onuayk, seyr uwr ma me lopa me ok mon me.” [Ais 35:5]
41008001	Enekwei meipey lwak ha lopa, uwrsa poya-poya homkwe ma-hokruw. Hom ayay lopa lwak menkin, Jisas hiykwe hyo ki-wayh me me-huonok nok, me,
41008002	“Hakwe uwrsa eme uron lowk, homkwe hane nion enekwei krompri sankaw lwak. Homkwe ayay lopa. [Mak 6:34-44]
41008003	Hakwe hme hmo a arian mon siowp nonaw me-ha ankin, homkwe yerki mon makuayk sakuayk nok ey, payhokuaw, hmo har homkwe meiaw-ar ko me le-nene.”
41008004	Hyo kiy-wayh hom lonuayk me, “Kipay uwrsa lopa erey mon kokwe, unsaney prueyn hiykwe uwrsa lowpwarowp eme kow-a ey hokwe, ihey mo naw perey suko se lonokyaw ey so?”
41008005	Jisas hiy hme mesopok, “Homkwe ihey mo naw pankaw mo?” Hom lonuayk me, “Iha sirom, mu nareysyar.”
41008006	Hiy uwrsa me ki mon me-wakiawk sir. Sei, hiykwe ihey mo naw iha sirom mu-nareysyar seme lonokyaw nok, God se nak-me-ihey nok, kamane nok, hyo ki-wayh me kow, uwrsa me lowndiy e. Hyo ki-wayh hom seseyn.
41008007	Homkwe seyr ay hu ko paswaw-neyney har non. Jisas hiykwe seyr seme nak-me-ihey nok, hyo ki-wayh me mekow, uwrsa me lowndiy e.
41008008	Uwrsa lowpwarowp homkwe swaw nuw-a mue. Sohiy so meyki hokwe, ki-wayh homkwe ayay kopi kopi mokwe yowr iha sirom mu nareysyar sankaw kawk kreik woki woki.
41008009	Uwrsa ma hokruw mo meir hokwe 4000 ohriar. Sa Jisas hiykwe hme me-ha nok,
41008010	hyo ki-wayh me nion yeyk mon lwawk nok, Dalmanuta mo kipay mon ley.
41008011	Farisi har hom le nok, Jisas se yier-ok non-me. Hye mon ir ey hokwe, homkwe hyekwe meir krai non, God hiy hye kar ma ley se mesair kow ey ke meio e mesopok.
41008012	Sawk Jisas hiykwe lenieys kawk nok, me, “Hai, uwrsa pokon ko homkwe, meir krai non me panoke mesopok o? Hakwe hme ok-ar kiy-mekow, uwrsa omokwe, meir krai non hme mesair kow ey liy kow ley.” [Mat 12:39; Luk 11:29]
41008013	Hiykwe sa hme lokriy hain nok, yeyk mon ma-lwawk nok, howk-menki mon ma-lokuan.
41008014	Ki-wayh homkwe uron lorionay. Homkwe ihey mo naw kraiar nake pa, sa hme nion kokwe yeyk mon kokwe, imon-awaw.
41008015	Jisas hiy hme me-kupaku, “Homkwe kwa ehei ehei, seyr Farisi mo yis o, Herot so yis o, seme iray iray non kwa lwak.” [Luk 12:1]
41008016	Hom homkiaw-ayay lohruw-a nok, me, “Hiykwe senkin sehe me, payhokuaw, hromkwe ihey mo naw lopa.”
41008017	Jisas hiykwe hom pay me lohruw-a e, hiykwe nonkway. Sa hiykwe hme sehe mesopok, “Homkwe ihey mo naw lopa ma lwak me panoke lohruw-a o? Hmey, homkwe korey nuw-ira pey, seyr korey nuw-nonkway pey? Hmey, hmo uron mokwe ku-mein lwak o? [Mak 6:52]
41008018	Homkwe nene non, sawk lira pey? Homkwe nweyk non, sawk lonuayk pey? Hmey, yor, paraw ha ma mon mokwe homkwe ma-nanpanan pey?
41008019	Enekwei ha ihey mo naw iha sirom me uwr 5000 me ma kamane kow, hai, ayay kopi kopi mokwe homkwe, yowr pankaw kawk woki woki mo?” Hom lonuayk me, “Iha seys, mu nareysyar.” [Mak 6:41-44]
41008020	“Seyr enekwei, ha ihey mo naw iha sirom mu nareysyar me uwrsa 4000 me ma kamane kow, hai, ayay kopi kopi mokwe homkwe yowr pankaw kawk woki woki mo?” Hom lonuayk me, “Iha sirom mu nareysyar.”
41008021	Hiy hme mesopok, “Hmey, homkwe peyr korey kiy-nuw-nonkway pey?”
41008022	Hom Betsaida mon lousne menkin, uwrsa har homkwe uwr prueyn nene kopyo se hiy-e nok, Jisas se lonseyn, uwr sehe sapou e.
41008023	Jisas hiykwe uwr nene kopyo sehe iha mon nekie nok nok, yier meykyay mon hiy-ey. Hiy uwr sohiy so nene mon somor kekie nok, hyo iha ke uwr sohiy so eir mon nak-kekie nok, kiy-nak-mesopok, “Hunkwe omeme har pankaw lira o?”
41008024	Uwr sohiy ar-ira nok, kiy-me, “Hakwe uwrsa me lira, sawk homkwe now hom lanio sayok me hieyn lira.”
41008025	Sei, Jisas hiy hyo iha me uwr sohiy so nene mon ma-kekie. Sa uwr sohiy so nene hom lon-kamapi, sa hiykwe ma-lira, seyr omeme lowpwarowp me yaprue nuw-ira hrahra ha.
41008026	Sohiy so meyki hokwe, Jisas hiykwe uwr sehe a mon senkin kiy-nak-me-sous kraipakrai ha, “Yier mon peie ma-lyawriy o.”
41008027	Sei, Jisas o, hyo ki-wayh o, homkwe yier, Sisaria Filipai ohriar mon ma lwak mon ley. Yerki mon kokwe, hiy hme mesopok, “Uwrsa homkwe hanekwe posokwaw ok me o?”
41008028	Hom lonuayk me, “Har homkwe senkin me, hunkwe Jon hu mon prouk uwr. Har homkwe senkin me, hunkwe Elaija, seyr har homkwe senkin me, hunkwe profet prueyn.” [Mak 6:15]
41008029	Hiy hme mesopok, “Hai, hom? Homkwe hanekwe posokwaw ok me o?” Pita hiy lonuayk me, “Hunkwe Krais.” [Mak 9:9; Jon 6:68-69]
41008030	Jisas hiy hye unsaney prueyn se mekow ame hme kiynak-me-kupaku.
41008031	Sei, Jisas hiy pa hyo ki-wayh me kiy-hiynuw-mon-sorasor, “Uwrsa mo Ney hiykwe aw kraiar nak-oum ey, seyr Juda mo uwr hakamay o, pris karmay o, sow ke hiymon sorasor uwr o, homkwe hye me-puar ey. Hyekwe ya lokin kwor okrue a, sawk eypok krompri so meyki hokwe, hiykwe su ma-loksian wayr ey.”
41008032	Hiykwe ok somokwe hmekwe kumay-ar nuw-mekow, sa Pita hiy hye huonok ohya nok, hye me-hripahri.
41008033	Sawk Jisas hiykwe lorok swakoum-sow nok, hyo ki-wayh me lira nok, Pita se me-hripahri. Hiy me, “Poup ara, hunkwe hano nene ko se kwa ley. Hno uron ko mokwe, God so mon le pey, sawk uwr so mon le.”
41008034	Sei, Jisas hiykwe uwrsa popua hay o, hyo ki-wayh o, hme me-huonok nok, kiy-me, “Unsaney prueyn hano meyki pyay e mon ankin, hiykwe hiykiaw-ayay lorionay nok, hyo now nak-okin pror kawk okrue ey se lway nok, hane pyay. [Mat 10:38-39; Luk 14:27]
41008035	Payhokuaw, unsaney hyo niohney se posokwaw nak-ono sous-a-sous e mon e, hiykwe hyo niohney se mon swakawk ha ey, sawk unsaney hyo niohney se hane hokuaw o, ok-ihey ke hokuaw o, posokwaw mon swakawk kow e, hiykwe hyo niohney se ma-lonok ey.
41008036	Sawk uwr prueyn hiykwe ki ohi so omeme lowpwarowp me nak-swakakar wayr ankin, sa hyo wa hokwe God se nak-nonkway pa lwak ankin, hai, omeme ki ko somokwe omok kokwe hyo wa se kokwe penkin hiymon ey so?
41008037	Seyr hiykwe hyo wa hokwe pay non manon-swawos onok a?
41008038	Enekwei ohokwe yor piap-araw non, seyr uwrsa homkwe God se nanpanan pey. Sa unsaney enekwei ohiy sok hane o, hano ok o, owh-mar posokwaw lon e, Uwrsa mo Ney hiykwe Aio so panpaniowni non hyo ensel pekneyweys me nion non-e ankin, hiykwe uwr sehe owh-mar lon ey.” [Mat 10:33]
41009001	Hiy hme makiy-me, “Hakwe hme ok-ar kiy-mekow, hmo har erey ma kiy-nakrok omokwe, lokrue lopa, hom God so Wayr-hre-yier, hiy krai non nake se lira sehe.” [Mak 13:30]
41009002	Eypok iha sirom pru non so meyki hokwe, Jisas hiykwe Pita o, Jems o, Jon o, hme huonok nok, mnuw meipey hay kamon mon hiy-iau. Serey kokwe homkwe homkiaw-aw lwak. Sa hmo inour mon kokwe, Jisas hiykwe irweyk-aw kiynuw-kahriy-sow.
41009003	Hyo owh ko omeme hom weyspey kiynuw-wak nak-oksa-nweyr-a-nweyr. Unsaney prueyn ki ko omeme seme weyspey-ar liy peyryapeyr ousne ley.
41009004	Sei, hom sa Elaija, Moses leys hoh Jisas se nion non-ohruw-a me lira.
41009005	Pita hiy Jisas se kiy-me, “Hiymon sorasor uwr ara, hrom erey ma kiy-wak omokwe, yaprue. Hromkwe ey-kroh krompri non meio ey. Kamon hno, kamon Moses so, kamon Elaija so.”
41009006	Pita hiykwe ok hiy me ey kokwe, nonkway lwak pa. Payhokuaw, homkwe nuw-hok krwepakrwe.
41009007	Sei, waw kamon hok lousne nok, Jisas o, Elaija, Moses leys o, hme swakuwmay. Sa wouk-ok kamon waw ko hokwe senkin me, “Ohokwe hano ney, hakwe hye uron-pi ko-ar nuw-wak. Hye lonuayk e.” [Ap 3:22; 2 Pi 1:17-18]
41009008	Ki-wayh hom saw-swahre-ahre ira, sawk homkwe unsaney prueyn lira pa; hme nion kokwe Jisas hiykwaw non-wak.
41009009	Hom mnuw se lokumey-sa-kumey menkin, Jisas hiy hme kiy-me-sous kraipakrai, “Hom pay me lira e, homkwe uwr prueyn se peie mekow o, Uwrsa mo Ney hiy lokrue ko se ma-loksian sehe.”
41009010	Homkwe sa hyo me-sous kraipakrai-ok ke lonuayk me, sawk homkiaw-aw kokwe ok “lokrue ko se ma-loksian” ko meyk-ar ke lohruw-a nanpanan.
41009011	Sa homkwe Jisas se mesopok, “Hai, sow ke hiymon sorasor uwr homkwe senkin panoke me o, Elaija hiykwe peyrmawk le ey?”
41009012	Jisas hiy lonuayk me, “Elaija hiykwe mo peyrmawk sehe le, omeme lowpwarowp me lonhan onhan koruay e. Hai, mamey porih hokwe sawk senkin panoke me ko, Uwrsa mo Ney hiykwe aw kraiar nak-ok ey, seyr hyekwe me-puar ey? [Sng 22:1-18; Ais 53:3; Mal 4:5]
41009013	Sawk hakwe hme senkin mekow, Elaija hiykwe po le, * sa uwrsa homkwe hye kokwe, hom penkin lon e nan e, senkin po lon, God so mamey porih hok hye ma lohruw-a ko liyliy-aw.” [Mat 11:14]
41009014	Hom ki-wayh har mo owh mon ma-lousne menkin, homkwe uwrsa popua hay hom hme awndiy kawk me ka-ira ne. Seyr sow ke hiymon sorasor uwr homkwe hme yier-ok non-me.
41009015	Uwrsa hom Jisas se lira huon menkin, homkwe nuw-preiryay, sa homkwe hye me-ihey-ok me e lonsau onsau.
41009016	Jisas hiy hyo ki-wayh me mesopok, “Homkwe uwr seme nion kokwe, yier-ok pay me lon-me o?”
41009017	Uwr prueyn uwrsa popua hay mo ompok ko hiy lonuayk me, “Hiymon sorasor uwr ara, hakwe hano ney se hno owh mon hiy-e. Hiykwe niohney piap-araw non, sa hiykwe ok liy lohruw-a ley.
41009018	Enekwei niohney piap-araw sohiy hye wanohyay mokwe, hyekwe ki mon lway swasow. Sawn homkwe hyo woki mon hruw-hruw-ay, seyr hiykwe nays nuwnak-peyk kon-kreik nok, owh hiy i nuw-nake ok. Hakwe hno ki-wayh me mesopok, niohney piap-araw sehe me-su ha e, sawk homkwe liy so.”
41009019	Jisas hiy lonuayk me, “Uwrsa nanpanan kiykiy-ay yor lopa ey. Hakwe hme nion kokwe enekwei pankaw non-wak e? Hakwe hmekwe ipan enekwei pankaw lon e? Ney sehe hano owh mon hiy-e e.”
41009020	Sa homkwe nyo sehe hyo owh mon sehe hiy-ey. Niohney piap-araw sohiy Jisas se lira menkin, hiy sa nyo sehe nuw-mon kowkow mon-ma-mon yay. Nyo sohokwe sa ki mon makuayk nokriy-a-nokriy merie merie, seyr sawn homkwe hyo woki mon hruw-hruw-ay.
41009021	Jisas hiy ney sohiy so orih se mesopok, “Hai, hiykwe senkin kokwe enekwei pankaw lwak so?” Hiy lonuayk me, “Hiy ney nopre kor-wak nonaw.
41009022	Enekwei kraiar niohney piap-araw sohokwe hyekwe ya mon lway swakawk, seyr hu mon lway swakeyn, hye lokin kwor e. Sawk hunkwe liy lwak ankin, hunkwe hreme uron kwa lowk, seyr hreme kwa hiymon.”
41009023	Jisas hiy hye makiy-mekow, “Hunkwe hanekwe ok senkin sokukwe panoke lohruw-a kow so ‘hunkwe liy lwak ankin’? Unsaney nan kiykiy-ay yor non hiykwe, omeme lowpwarowp mokwe hiykwe liy mon.” [Mat 21:21; Mak 11:23]
41009024	Peypey pa, ney sohiy so orih hiy sa senkin kiynuw-okre me, “Hakwe mo nan kiykiy-ay, sawk aiopey hay korey. Hano nan kiykiy-ay yor ke aiopey hay hiy-mon wak e.”
41009025	Jisas hiy uwrsa kraiar hom hme awndiy kawk me lira menkin, hiykwe sa niohney piap-araw se me-hripahri. Hiy me, “Niohney nweyk-saw lopa, seyr woki-ok lopa, hakwe hne kiy-me-kupaku, nyo sohiy so owh ko se ar-ousne ha e, seyr hyo mon peie ma-lyawriy o.”
41009026	Niohney piap-araw sohiy nuw-weyr-weyr nok, nyo sehe nuw-mon koukou piap-ma-piap nok, lousne. Nyo sohokwe sopok se hieyn-aw lira, sa uwrsa lowpwarowp homkwe senkin me, “Hiykwe papo lokrue.” [Mak 1:26]
41009027	Sawk Jisas hiy hye iha mon nekie nok, hye lway sian, sa hiykwe sehe loksian orok.
41009028	Jisas hiy a mon ma lyawriy so meyki hokwe, hyo ki-wayh homkwe hye ouon-aw mesopok, “Hai, hromkwe niohney sehe me-su ha pa panoke lwak mo?”
41009029	Hiy lonuayk me, “Senkin somokwe God se mesopok yor nonaw me-su ha.”
41009030	Homkwe yier sehe lokriy hain nok, sa Galili mo kipay mon ley hain. Jisas hiykwe hom perey lwak e, unsaney prueyn nonkway e mon pa, [Jon 7:1]
41009031	payhokuaw, hiykwe hyo ki-wayh me hiymon sorasor. Hiy hme me, “Uwrsa mo Ney se kokwe, awia mo iha mon kow ey, sa homkwe hye lokin kwor ey. Sa eypok krompri so meyki hokwe, hiykwe ma-loksian ey.” [Mak 8:31; 10:32-34]
41009032	Sawk homkwe hyo ok-ku kokwe nonkway pa, seyr homkwe nak-hok, hyekwe mesopok pa. [Luk 9:45]
41009033	Hom Kaperneam mon lousne, sa hiy a mon lwak menkin, Jisas hiykwe hyo ki-wayh me pa kiy-mesopok. “Homkwe yerki mon kokwe pay me lon-seyrpaseyr ne mo?”
41009034	Sawk homkwe hye liy ma-sahre onuayk me e ko, payhokuaw, homkwe yerki mon kokwe peyrmawk posokwaw lwak e, seme homkiaw-ayay lon-seyrpaseyr ne.
41009035	Jisas hiy kiy-iwak nok, hyo ki-wayh iha seys mu nareysyar me ka-me-huonok nok, kiy-me, “Unsaney peyrmawk lwak e posokwaw mon e, hiykwe lowpwarowp mo pariawey-ar kwa lwak, seyr lowpwarowp mo mey-uwr puraw kwa lwak.” [Mat 20:25-27; Mak 10:43-44; Luk 22:24]
41009036	Hiykwe ney prueyn huonok nok, hmo ompok mon kiy-mon iarok. Hiykwe ney sehe nweyh kane kawk nok, hme kiynak-me,
41009037	“Unsaney, ney ohom mo prueyn se hano uru non posokwaw me-huonok yawriy e, hiykwe hane me-huonok yawriy. Seyr hane posokwaw me-huonok yawriy e, hiykwe hane-aw me-huonok yawriy pey, sawk uwr hane ma me-ha o.” [Mat 10:40]
41009038	Jon hiy me, “Hiymon sorasor uwr ara, hromkwe uwr prueyn niohney piap-araw me hno uru non me-su ha me lira, sa hromkwe hye me-sous, payhokuaw, hiykwe hromo prueyn korey.”
41009039	Jisas hiy hme mekow, “Hye peie me-sous o, payhokuaw, uwr prueyn meir krai non hano uru non ma meio hiykwe, hane ok-piap-ok liy makiy-saw-me ley.
41009040	Payhokuaw, unsaney hreme aw lono pa lwak ankin, hiykwe hromo. [Mat 12:30; Luk 11:23]
41009041	Hakwe hme okar kiy-mekow, hom Krais so ma lwak me hokuaw, unsaney hme hu yiawk non hano uru non posokwaw kow owswa e, hiykwe pie ya lonok a.” [Mat 10:42]
41009042	“Sawk unsaney har homkwe unsaney, ney ehe hieyn hane ma nan kiykiy-ay me mon-kuayk ankin, uwrsa senkin somokwe yor piap-araw aiopey hay ke nuw-mon. Me o, uwr senkin sohokwe sour-yawp-ar mon paraw mein aiopey hay non huei sok nuw-piynay swakeyn omprok ha lak pok.
41009043	Hno iha hok hne weyn piap-araw mon meio ankin, hunkwe kwa lokiane sow. Hwon God so Wayr-hre-yier mon iha kamon-aw nak-yawriy hokwe, yaprue, sawk Satan so yier, ya ma pros lopa mon iha kreys non nak-yawriy hokwe, piap-araw. [
41009044	‘Satan so yier sohokwe kiohno hme ma la homkwe seyn lokrue pey, seyr ya hokwe seyn mon pros pey.’] [Mat 5:30]
41009045	Seyr hno sune hok hne weyn piap-araw ke mon meio ankin, hunkwe kwa lokiane sow. Hwon God so Wayr-hre-yier mon sune kamon-aw nak-yawriy hokwe, yaprue, sawk hne Satan so yier mon sune kreys non nak-way swakawk hokwe piap-araw. [
41009046	‘Satan so yier sohokwe kiohno hme ma la homkwe seyn lokrue pey, seyr ya hokwe seyn pros pey.’]
41009047	Sa hno nene hiy hne weyn piap-araw ke mon meio ankin, hunkwe kwa kair. Hwon God so yier mon nene namon-aw nak-yawriy hokwe, yaprue, sawk hne Satan so yier mon nene nareys non nak-way swakawk hokwe, piap-araw. [Mat 5:29]
41009048	‘Satan so yier sohokwe kiohno hme ma la homkwe seyn lokrue pey, seyr ya hokwe seyn pros pey.’
41009049	Seyr uwrsa me kokwe ya hok nuw-oum mnow-mnow ihey ey, ayay naws prawk kow ey me sol non ma mon mnow-mnow ihey senkin.
41009050	Sol mokwe yaprue, sawk sol hokwe wonor lwak pa lwak ankin, hai, homkwe penkin ma-mon wonor o? Homkwe wayh-wayh me nion non-wawwaw sol non kwa lwak, seyr wayh-wayh me nion aymarowh-aw kwa non-wayr.” [Mat 5:13; Luk 14:34]
41010001	Sei, Jisas hiykwe yier sehe lokriy hain nok, sa Judia mo kipay mon ley, yawp Jordan se kuan iau. Uwrsa popua hay homkwe hyo owh mon ma-le nene. Sa hiykwe hme hiymon sorasor, hiy ma lon wayr-wayr senkin.
41010002	Farisi har hom le nok, hye mon-ir ey hokwe homkwe senkin mesopok, “Hreme mekow e, hromo sow hokwe uwr prueyn hyo sah ke me-su ha e ipan pankaw lon o?”
41010003	Jisas hiykwe sa mesopok non ma-sahre onuayk me, “Hai, Moses hiykwe hmekwe sow penkin ke kow so?”
41010004	Hom me, “Moses hiykwe uwr prueyn, hiy hyo sah ke me-su ha mamey non nak-me-su ha ey hokwe ipan lon.”
41010005	Jisas hiy ma-sahre onuayk me, “Moses hiykwe hmekwe sow sokukwe sehe mey kow, payhokuaw, hmo uron mokwe ku-mein lwak.
41010006	Sawk omeme lowpwarowp me ma monhre pie hokwe, God hiykwe ‘iwar me kokwe, uwr o, sa o, senkin monhre.’
41010007	‘Meyk sohiy so hokuaw kokwe, uwr hiykwe hyo aio ipey me lokriy hain nok, hyo sah ke nion non-okin nasay ok,
41010008	sa hohkwe owhi kamon-aw non-wak.’ Hohkwe prueys manon-wak pey, sawk kamon-aw.
41010009	Sohiy so hokuaw kokwe, God hiy payay se non-saronay e, uwr prueyn hiykwe irweyk irweyk-aw peie ma-mon wak o.”
41010010	Sa omok hom a mon ma-lwak menkin, ki-wayh homkwe hye ok sokwe mesopok.
41010011	Hiy lonuayk me, “Uwr prueyn hyo sah ke ma me-su ha hiykwe, sa prueyn ma-huon ankin, hiykwe hyo sah ke yokun nweyh kane yor ke mon. [Mat 5:32]
41010012	Liyliy-aw, sa prueyn hoko uruh se ma me-su ha hokwe, uwr prueyn ma-liwak ankin, hokwe yokun nweyh kane yor ke mon.”
41010013	Uwrsa homkwe ney nopre me Jisas so owh mon hiy-e, hiy hme hiy-nekie mesopok e. Sawk hmekwe ki-wayh hom me-hripahri.
41010014	Jisas hiy senkin lira menkin, hiykwe kasaw nuw-hohuaw. Hiy ki-wayh me me, “Ney nopre me hano owh mon ki-isay ha e, peie me-sous o, payhokuaw God so Wayr-hre-yier hokwe ney nopre senkin mo.
41010015	Hakwe hme ok-ar kiy-mekow, unsaney prueyn God so Wayr-hre-yier se ney nopre se hieyn lonok pa lwak ankin, hiykwe liy lyawriy ley.” [Mat 18:3]
41010016	Hiykwe sa ney seme nekie lar nok, hyo iha me hmo prueyn prueyn-aw mo eir mon kekie sowkriy nok, God so hiymon yor ke hiy-nekie mesopok.
41010017	Jisas hiy ma-ley liok menkin, uwr prueyn hiykwe hyo owh mon sau ne nok, hyo inour mon pamuow kampueys nok, hye mesopok, “Hiymon sorasor uwr yaprue ara, ha lwayr peyow ey se lonok ey hokwe, hakwe penkin lon e?”
41010018	Jisas hiy lonuayk me, “Hai, hunkwe hane kokwe yaprue-ok panoke me o? Uwr prueyn yaprue lopa, God hiykwaw.
41010019	Hunkwe me-kupaku-ok mokwe nonkway: ‘Unsaney peie lokin kwor okrue o, yokun peie nweyh kane o, yokun peie lopri o, har me okrei, uron-saw-ok non peie lokin lor-a-lor kow o, har mo omeme me okrei yor non ouon-aw peie me-warei-arei onok o, hno aio ipey me kwa nan ihey.’”
41010020	Uwr sohiy me, “Hiymon sorasor uwr ara, me-kupaku-ok somokwe hakwe ney nopre kor-wak nonaw nuw-pyay ne.”
41010021	Jisas hiykwe hye uron-pi ko-ar non nuwnak-ira nok, me, “Hunkwe yor kamon kokwe ohna lwak. Hunkwe ley nok, hno omeme lowpwarowp me isay nakway nok, mein-owon seme uwrsa omeme lopa me kow. Sa nonkumey mon kokwe hunkwe omeme kraiar non lwak ey. Senkin lon nok, hano meyki nak-pyay.”
41010022	Uwr sohokwe ok seme lonuayk menkin, hiykwe ine kasaw nuw-ey-kwopakwo nok. Hiy ma ley hokwe, hiykwe uron nuw-owk nok, payhokuaw, hiykwe omeme kraiar non.
41010023	Jisas hiykwe hyo ki-wayh me lira sahre-ahre nok, hme kiy-me, “Uwr omeme kraiar non hiy God so Wayr-hre-yier mon lyawriy ey hokwe, honon honon nuw-wak ey.”
41010024	Ki-wayh hom ok seme lonuayk menkin, homkwe nuw-preiryay. Sawk Jisas hiy ma-me, “Hano ney om, God so Wayr-hre-yier mon lyawriy ey hokwe honon honon.
41010025	Huok kamon, kamel-ok ma me, hiykwe ku-i omeme nak-pror ey so saw nopre mon lyawriy e mon ankin, hyekwe honon honon. Sawk uwr omeme kraiar non hiykwe seyr God so Wayr-hre-yier mon lyawriy e mon ankin, hyekwe honon honon-ar nuw-wak.”
41010026	Ki-wayh hom ok seme lonuayk menkin, homkwe ipey-ar nuw-preiryay. Sa homkiaw-ayay senkin lohruw-a, “Hai, sa uwr penkin me huonok prosue ey mo?”
41010027	Jisas hiy hme lira nok, kiy-me, “Uwr me kokwe sohokwe liy so, sawk God se kokwe honon honon korey, mey lowpwarowp mokwe God hiykwe liy.”
41010028	Pita hiy Jisas se kiy-me, “Hromkwe omeme lowpwarowp po lokriy hain, hne pyay e.”
41010029	Jisas hiy lonuayk me, “Hakwe hme okar kiy-mekow, unsaney prueyn hyo a, oryay, ine, ipey, aio, ney, wueir, seme hane hokuaw, seyr ok-ihey ke hokuaw lokriy hain ankin,
41010030	hiykwe enekwei ohokwe kraiar-ar ma-sahre onok ey. Hiykwe a, oryay, ine, ipey, ney, wueir, seyr low o, somokwe kraiar-ar ma-sahre onok ey, sankaw 100. Seyr enekwei omok kokwe hiykwe lwayr peyow ey se lonok ey.
41010031	Sawk uwrsa kraiar peyrmawk ma lwak homkwe, pariawey-ar lwak ey, sa pariawey ma lwak homkwe peyrmawk lwak ey.” [Mat 20:16; Luk 13:30]
41010032	Jisas o, hyo ki-wayh o, homkwe yerki Jerusalem mon ma liau mon lwak. Jisas hiykwe hmo peyrmawk liarok. Ki-wayh homkwe kraiar nanpanan, seyr uwrsa meyki ma pyay homkwe nuw-hok. Jisas hiy hyo ki-wayh iha seys mu nareysyar me nian-aw huonok nok, weynpaweyn hye lousne ey me mesor kow.
41010033	Jisas hiy me, “Kwa lonuayk, hromkwe Jerusalem mon liau. Sa Uwrsa mo Ney se kokwe, pris karmay o, sow ke hiymon-sorasor uwr o, hmo iha mon kow ey. Homkwe hye lokin kwor ey se nuw-ohruw-a sakon kawk nok, hye uwrkayn irweyk mo iha mon kow ok.
41010034	Uwrkayn irweyk homkwe hye lourde nok, somor somor say kow nok, lomniy nok, lokin kwor okrue ok. Sawk eypok krompri so meyki hokwe, hiykwe su ma-loksian wayr ey.” [Mak 8:31; 9:31]
41010035	Sebedi so ney prueysyar, Jems, Jon leys hohkwe hyo owh mon le nok, me, “Hiymon sorasor uwr ara, hrorkwe hne hror pay me mesopok e, hwon senkin lon e mon.”
41010036	Jisas hiy hme kiy-mesopok, “Hai, hohkwe ha hehe pay me lon kow e me o?”
41010037	Hoh lonuayk me, “Enekwei hwon hno sia-king hno Wayr-hre-yier panpaniowni non mon ma lwak mon liwak ankin, hunkwe hrerekwe prueyn sayar mon, prueyn irayh mon, senkin isay iwak e.”
41010038	Jisas hiy hme me, “Hohkwe hoh pay se mesopok e, nonkway lwak pey. Hai, hohkwe yiawk ha lowswa ey hokwe, liy lowswa o? Hai, hohkwe hane prouk ey, senkin liy prouk o?” [Mak 14:36; Luk 12:50]
41010039	Hoh lonuayk me, “Hrorkwe liy.” Jisas hiy hehe me, “Okar, yiawk ha lowswa ey hokwe, hohkwe seyr ya non-owswa a. Seyr hehekwe hane prouk ey, senkin ya prouk a. [Ap 12:2; MHO 1:9]
41010040	Sawk hakwe uru lopa, unsaney hano sayar mon liwak ey o, hano irayh mon liwak ey o, seme liaup ey hokwe. Yop somokwe uwrsa God hiykiaw ma lonhan kow koruay mo.”
41010041	Ki-wayh iha seys hom senkin lonuayk menkin, homkwe sa Jems, Jon leys se kasaw nuw-hohuaw.
41010042	Jisas hiy hme lowpwarowp me swa-hokruw nok, kiy-me, “Homkwe nonkway, haiden homkwe uwr hmo hiy-wayr uwr-ok ma me so krai ouon mon lwak, seyr hmo peyrmawk liarok uwr homkwe hiy-wayr krai lowpwarowp non. [Luk 22:25-26]
41010043	Sawk hmo ompok mon kokwe senkin lwak pey. Uwr hmo ompok mon uru aiopey hay non posokwaw lwak e mon e, hiykwe hmo mey-uwr puraw kwa lwak. [Mat 23:11; Mak 9:35]
41010044	Seyr uwr peyrmawk lwak e posokwaw mon e, hiykwe lowpwarowp mo mey-uwr puraw kwa lwak kow.
41010045	Payhokuaw, Uwrsa mo Ney hiykwe sehe le pa, uwrsa hom hyo mey me meio kow e. Sawk hiykwe sehe le, hiykwaw uwrsa me meio kow e, seyr hiykiaw-ayay uwrsa kraiar me pie se hieyn nakway preisia ha e.”
41010046	Sei, hom sa Jeriko mon le. Jisas o, hyo ki-wayh o, uwrsa popua hay o, hom yier aiopey hay sehe kiy-okriy hain nonaw, uwr prueyn nene kopyo Bartimeus-ok ma me, Timeus so ney hiykwe yerki meykyay mon wakiawk lonseyn.
41010047	Bartimeus hiy senkin lonuayk menkin, uwr sohokwe Jisas Nasaret ko, hiy pau ok aiopey hay kiynuw-okre me, “Jisas, Devit so Ney, hane uron lowk e.”
